Recruiting Shop Turns Out to be a Bandit Den, Three Girls Almost Sold

Around 5 pm the day before yesterday, Zhong Yuting, a guard at the Nanxiang station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Motor Road, discovered five suspicious male and female travelers. After taking them to the bureau, the director of the Zheng Branch Bureau interrogated them. The man claimed to be Hong Yuhe from Yangzhou, who runs a recruiting shop on Tangshan Road in Hongkou, Shanghai. The women were: Lin Jinbao, 25 years old, from Zhenjiang, who runs a barbershop on Gao Langqiao in Shanghai; Li Jinmei, 20 years old, from Tongzhou, who lives in Bada Alley on Yangzhou Road in Shanghai; Wang Sanmei, 20 years old, from Yancheng, who lives in Yangshupu in Shanghai; and Zhao Zhaodi, 18 years old, from Tongzhou, who lives with Li Jinmei. He also claimed that they were deceived by Hong Yuhe and Lin Jinbao on the 14th of the lunar month and initially lived in the Zhongnan Hotel in Shanghai, under the name Wang Weide. On the fourth day, they went to the home of Hong's relative in Zhengjia Muqiao. They only stayed one night because the family saw that their actions were improper and kicked them out. So, from the fifth day, they stayed in the Jiaotong Hotel, and also stayed for three nights. Then they opened the Hongkou Zhongshan Hotel, under the pseudonym Zhang Zaisan. Lin Jinbao also confessed that the three girls were from a yarn factory and he knew it. Hong Yuhe asked me to lead them out to play. When opening the hotel, it was not only Hong alone. Most of the men took turns to sleep with them. Yesterday (the day before yesterday), they took a small train to Nanxiang, intending to transfer to Suzhou. The three girls also said that they were deceived by Lin Jinbao, saying that they would work in the factory, but they were deceived. After checking the confession, Director Zheng believed that the case was criminal and involved the suspicion of obstructing morality and seducing others to leave their families. It was not enough to strictly investigate. So, he specially summoned the families of the three girls yesterday and interrogated them. Around 6 pm yesterday, he took them to the Jiading County Government for interrogation. According to Lin Jinbao's confession, when they were arrested at Nanxiang Station, there was another man named Mao Wanyu who escaped. Mao is the main criminal who designed to deceive the three girls to Suzhou for sale.

Ni Heting from Ningbo is blind in one eye, so he works as a fortune teller. His daughter, Yunmei, is also blind in one eye, and her husband, Fu Atang, is blind in both eyes and works in the same industry as his father-in-law. Recently, Ni Heting suddenly accused Qiao Hongkui, a fellow villager living at No. 307 Yuezhou Road, of raping his daughter Yunmei. The court has completed the interrogation of the case. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhong Qing took the seat in Criminal Court II and announced the verdict: Qiao Hongkui was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for raping a girl who was over 14 and under 16 years old.

Feng Baishun, a Chinese detective from the Chengdu Road Patrol, and Wang Yongjun, a detective, found out about it. Qian Xunjiu, a lawyer from the Shanghai Municipal Council, filed a public lawsuit against Fu Xingmao, the owner of the silver shop, on charges of receiving stolen goods and violating Article 34 of the Yangjing Hong Charter and Article 5 of the Silver Shop License Charter. Fu Xingmao arrived in court with his defense lawyer, Jiang Yiping. He submitted account books to prove that the gold jewelry received was not lower than the market price. After being transferred to the court for verification, the lawyers of both parties were asked to debate, and the verdict was announced in court: Fu Xingmao was acquitted of the charge of receiving stolen goods. He was fined 50 yuan for the charge of violating regulations.

Domestic Wheat Bumper Harvest, Reduced Imports of Foreign Wheat

This year, Su, Wan, Yu, and E provinces have a bumper harvest of wheat, with wheat production increasing by 30 to 40 percent compared to previous years. The market price is also extremely stable, generally between four yuan and forty-five cents per pound. According to sources in the grain industry, flour mills in this city, in view of the high market price of foreign wheat and the large price difference with domestic wheat, are enthusiastically purchasing domestic wheat in various places. The number of established outlets is also more than in previous years. Foreign wheat is being rejected and not purchased. It is expected that if there are no special changes, imports of foreign wheat this year will be greatly reduced.

National Goods Association Requests Exemption from Inspection of Domestically Produced Electrical Appliances

The Shanghai National Goods Factories Joint Association sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office yesterday, stating that according to a letter from its member, the Huatong Electrical Machinery Factory, due to the increasing smuggling activities, the Customs has set up inspection offices at railway stations to inspect incoming and outgoing goods. The factory's products shipped from Shanghai to various locations via the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways must be inspected and released, which causes delays. Currently, it is the peak season for fan sales, and managers in various ports are in urgent need. They find this procedure quite difficult. Since the factory's products are entirely domestically produced, it requests exemption from inspection. Three copies of the trademark design are enclosed for verification by your association to confirm they are indeed domestic products and request approval for their release. It is noted that the factory specializes in manufacturing AC and DC generators, high and low voltage panels, various automatic oil switches, voltage testers, various electrical appliances for trains, electric furnaces, electric ovens, electric stoves, DC and AC electric fans, and various industrial electrical machinery. Its products are of excellent quality and are operated with domestic capital, which is sufficient to resist the invasion of imported goods. Therefore, protection is necessary. This letter is to certify and request your office to order the railway station inspection office to exempt these goods from inspection to facilitate transportation and safeguard domestic products.

Zhang Shen Returns from Studying Abroad, Arrives in Shanghai by Ship Yesterday

Zhang Zhong, courtesy name Minyang, is a native of Lin'an, Zhejiang. He obtained a bachelor's degree in education from Tokyo University in the 14th year of the Republic of China. He served as a supervisor in Beijing and held important positions in the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau for a total of eight years. On July 10, 1934, he went to England for self-funded study, enrolling in the Royal College of Education at the University of London to study educational administration. In January 1935, he transferred to the University of Michigan in the United States to continue his studies in educational administration. He also traveled extensively to various places for detailed observation. He obtained a master's degree in June and boarded the Canadian Empress ship on the 27th to return to China. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the 14th), and relatives and friends from afar went to the ship to welcome him.

China International Famine Relief Commission's Last Year's Cooperation, Training, and Instruction

The China International Famine Relief Commission, located at 505 Henan Road, is dedicated to disaster prevention and mitigation. In addition to roads and water conservancy projects, it also promotes rural cooperation to benefit people's livelihoods. The cooperative societies sponsored and guided by the commission have now reached over 10,000 across the country. Hebei Province is the first pilot area, with numerous cooperative affairs. Over 2,000 cooperative societies have been established. Cooperative training courses, instructor training classes, and special training classes are held in various parts of the province to popularize cooperative knowledge. The following is a summary of the cooperative training and instruction organized by the commission in Hebei Province last year: (1) Cooperative Training Courses: (Eleventh Session) Aimed at training cooperative talents, these courses are organized by various joint societies and cooperative societies. Last year, there were 92 groups distributed in 59 counties in Hebei Province, with a total of 6,722 trainees representing 1,873 cooperative societies. The total cost was $1,538.75. (2) Instructor Training Classes: Aimed at cultivating instructors for training, these classes are organized by county joint societies. There were eight groups in Shenze, Pingxiang, Lecheng, Anping, Hejian, Wuji, Feixiang, Jin County, etc., with over 200 trainees. (3) Special Training Classes: Also aimed at training cooperative talents, these classes are specifically for newly established cooperative societies in flood-stricken areas because they lack the ability to organize on their own. The commission assigns locations and sends personnel to handle them on their behalf. These members are trained through special training classes. There were two groups in Puyang County, with 157 participants representing 88 cooperative societies. The total cost was $23.59.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The 291st Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of Central Bank Exchange Certificates states: In accordance with Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the amount of exchange certificates issued by the bank and the reserve funds. We conducted the 291st inspection at the Issuance Bureau of the bank on July 11, 1936. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange certificates issued is 30,548,343 yuan in silver, including 27,418,6939 yuan in silver yuan certificates and 3,129,6504 yuan in fractional currency certificates. The total amount of exchange certificate reserve funds is 30,548,343 yuan, including 20,711,2143 yuan in cash reserve in silver. The cash reserve is deposited as follows: 10,326,9477 yuan and 18 cents are deposited in the bank's issuing branches and sub-branches, and 10,374,2665 yuan and 82 cents are deposited in peer banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 9,837,1300 yuan in silver. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange certificates issued is 400,963.07 yuan. The total amount of customs gold exchange certificate reserve funds is 400,963.07 yuan. The reserve fund includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, totaling 400,962.07 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the remainder should be guaranteed by legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is submitted on July 12, 1936. Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank: Li Fuxun, Supervisors: Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jili.

Sujia Road Opens to Traffic Today

The Sujia Railway, commissioned by the Ministry of Railways to be built by the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, was completed last month and is scheduled to officially open to traffic today and sell passenger tickets. The two bureau chiefs, Huang Boqiao, are scheduled to inspect the road with the chiefs of various departments this morning. A special train will depart from Shanghai at 4:45 AM to Suzhou, and then transfer to the first train to Jiaxing to inspect the entire line. The first train from Jiaxing to Suzhou will depart at 7:00 AM. To commemorate the opening of the railway, passengers who purchase one-way tickets within five days will have a commemorative stamp affixed, and the return fare will be waived during these five days. However, there will be no ceremony at the opening of the railway.

Patrol Officer Long Jianpo Faces Another Lawsuit

Patrol Officer Long Jianpo of the Xinchan Branch was previously accused by Wu Xiaosan of Funing of being arrested because Patrol Leader Xue Zheng and Police Officer Wen Shiying, subordinates of Patrol Officer Long, demanded gratuities from the Huayanglou Teahouse and were unsuccessful. Wu Xiaosan intervened and was arrested. He requested that Xue Zheng and Wen Shiying be investigated according to the law. As a result, Xue Zheng was found not guilty, and Wen Shiying was sentenced to 59 days of detention and given a suspended sentence. However, Long Jianpo was not a defendant at the time, but there were letters and testimonies in which Patrol Officer Long assigned police chiefs to solicit gratuities. Therefore, Long believed that he was falsely accused and that his reputation was harmed. He filed a lawsuit with the Prosecutor's Office. Wu Xiaosan was ordered to post bail, and Wu Xiaosan submitted counter-evidence, requesting an investigation into whether shops within the jurisdiction of the Xinchan Branch had been extorted for gratuities. After reviewing the case, Prosecutor Lei Binzhang believed that a thorough investigation was necessary. Therefore, he personally investigated and found that 40 to 50 shops had paid gratuities. He then obtained several account books and, according to his prosecutorial authority, reported the matter. Yesterday, he ordered Long Jianpo to be summoned to court and ordered him to post bail pending investigation. While the Prosecutor's Office was still investigating, Wu Renfu of Funing accused Long Jianpo of abuse of power and illegal detention. He stated that it was related to Wu Xiaosan's case, and because Wu Xiaosan cited him as a witness, Patrol Officer Long held a grudge and used his position and authority to arrest him. He cited Chen Dexing, Wang Zanyao, and Zhang Songlin as witnesses. Yesterday, Judge Li questioned Long, who denied the detention. Lawyer Ji Fenglv, representing the defense, argued that the witnesses had made false statements and requested a confrontation. The judge adjourned the hearing.

Saving Exported Egg Products: International Trade Bureau Considers Measures

Egg products are a major export from our country, and have become even more significant in recent years. Last year, eggs and egg products ranked third among the major export goods. The main destination for these exports is the United Kingdom, followed by Germany, and then the United States. However, judging from trade trends, the sales in the UK have been declining year by year, as is the case with Germany. Furthermore, Germany has recently implemented economic controls and foreign exchange management, which may further hinder egg product sales. However, the sales in the United States have slightly reversed the downward trend in recent years. Although the eggs and egg products shipped to the United States last year increased by three and a half times compared to the previous year, they are still inferior to those of three or four years ago. However, the market for egg products is primarily based in the United Kingdom and the United States. In recent years, the United Kingdom and the United States have become wary of the activity of our country's egg products and are actively trying to develop their domestic production capacity and restrict the progress of our country's egg products. For example, the United States plans to increase import tariffs, and British merchants are vigorously promoting the poor quality of our country's egg products, advocating a ban on imports or increased taxes to restrict them. Although the British government is mindful of diplomatic relations and has not yet adopted these measures, the British promotion is persistent, and the future is worrying. Even if the British government does not temporarily increase taxes, the sales of our country's egg products may inevitably be affected. This trend can be observed in the reduced export of egg products to the UK in the past two years. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce is paying close attention to this matter. In addition to informing the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct ambassadors abroad to pay attention at all times, it has also ordered the International Trade Bureau to actively plan for relief measures. At the same time, the Sino-British Trade Association, jointly formed by the Shanghai British Chamber of Commerce and the China International Trade Association, is also paying attention to this matter in order to promote Sino-British trade. It has discussed and formulated five improvement measures and submitted them to the ministry for assessment. The main points are summarized as follows: Research and Improvement: Representatives from the Egg Industry Association, the Commodity Inspection Bureau, and the Sino-British Trade Association will be elected to form an Egg Products Improvement Committee. Experts will be hired to set up venues to study and promote the improvement of chicken breeds and increase production. At the same time, guidance on feeding and disease prevention will be implemented. In addition to the contributions from the above-mentioned agencies, the government should subsidize a monthly amount, similar to the China United Sericulture Improvement Association. Education and Promotion: This work is currently being carried out by private individuals. The strength is weak, and the effect is naturally small. In the future, publications should be increased, with simple language to describe feeding and disease prevention methods, and spread to the people, so that they know how to improve.

There Was Thunder and Rain in the City Yesterday, with Thunder and Lightning Lasting for a Long Time Before Stopping. The Rain, Longed For, Greatly Benefits Agriculture.

According to Datong Du Yun, the weather in this city was the hottest on the 11th since the beginning of summer, with the temperature rising to over 97 degrees. However, starting the next day, it suddenly cooled down again, and the wind blew fiercely all day long. This deep coolness lasted until the night before last. Yesterday morning, the weather gradually warmed up, but around 1 PM, thunder and lightning suddenly occurred, and heavy rain poured down. The thunder stopped at 5 PM, and the rain also stopped. In the evening, the sky was still cloudy and uncertain. Since the beginning of summer this year, the rainfall has been scarce, and the heat has recently been intense, with drought gradually emerging. Farmers are longing for rain, which is extremely urgent. Therefore, yesterday's timely rain greatly benefited agriculture. Propaganda Towards Britain: In order to stop the export of egg products from various countries to the UK, British egg merchants have organized a campaign of destructive propaganda, which has greatly affected the export of Chinese eggs to the UK. Although this propaganda has temporarily stopped in recent years, our country must actively promote our products. The government should publish English pamphlets explaining the cleanliness of Chinese egg factories and the completeness of the inspection work. In addition, the process from chicken raising in rural areas to egg product export should be filmed and screened at gatherings of British civil society organizations. The power of publicity will be great, and the effectiveness can be imagined.

Tax Reductions and Exemptions: Export tariffs in our country are one of the sources of national revenue. In this time of financial difficulty, it is difficult to waive them all. However, it is found that eggs transported from Wuhu to Shanghai have already been taxed. After these eggs arrive in Shanghai, they are converted into liquid, packed, and exported, and the Shanghai Customs still charges export taxes. This system of one goods taxed twice should be changed. In the future, when national tax revenues are slightly more abundant, export taxes should be eliminated to facilitate foreign trade.

Expanded Inspection: In addition to chemical methods to analyze the contents of egg products, the inspection of egg factories is also very important. Currently, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau only inspects egg factories in Shanghai. Due to the long distance, egg factories in the interior have not been included in the inspection scope. In the future, they should also be subject to inspection, so that it will be more powerful to promote the cleanliness of our country's egg products abroad. After the Ministry of Industry and Commerce accepted the above articles, it ordered the International Trade Bureau to consult with all parties concerned and discuss practical and feasible measures. After the bureau negotiated with all parties, it convened egg manufacturers to study in detail. There has been a clue about the above five items. In the future, the export of egg products will be able to increase a lot of strength. As for the United States, there have also been recent discussions on raising the issue of egg products. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce has transferred the issue to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, ordering the ambassador to the United States to negotiate properly. The bureau also gathered major egg merchants such as Zheng Paixing, Tang Dingchen, and Wang Xinzai to discuss remedial and coping methods. It is said that there are considerable ways to go.

Chaozhou Native Association Commemorates Zheng Zhengqiu

The late Chairman Zheng Zhengqiu of the Chaozhou Native Association in Shanghai, in his lifetime, not only devoted himself to the arts but also was enthusiastic about social undertakings. He held numerous important public positions in various organizations. He spared no effort in advocating public welfare, dedicating himself to the cause. He served as the chairman of the Chaozhou Native Association in Shanghai for four years, leading the association's affairs and being courageous in taking responsibility. The Chaozhou people in Shanghai all admired him. The association's achievements today are largely due to his contributions. Since his passing last summer, a year has quickly passed. July 16th is the anniversary of Mr. Zheng's death. In order to commemorate his merits and remember the past, the association specially decided through a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members to designate this day as "Chairman Zheng's Memorial Day," and to hold a memorial ceremony every year to preserve his memory permanently. It is also decided to hold the "Memorial Meeting for the First Anniversary of the Death of the Late Chairman Zheng" at 4 p.m. on the 16th of this month at the association's premises on Xizilaihuo Street. Fellow villagers are welcome to participate freely. After the meeting, they plan to discuss the preparations for a public burial, so that they can start the process. As for the anniversary memorial for the family and former friends, it is heard that it will be held separately at another location on the sixteenth day of the sixth month of the lunar calendar, the anniversary of his death.

Liu Haisu Art Exhibition Extended for Three Days

Since the opening of Liu Haisu's art exhibition on the first of this month, it has been extremely popular with visitors. From the first to the fifth, there were more than 4,000 visitors each day. From the sixth to the twelfth, due to the hot weather, the daily average was also around 700 people. In the past two days, the stifling heat has turned cooler, and visitors have become crowded again. Due to the hot weather, the association has installed electric fans and distributed cool air to regulate the temperature. Because those who come to visit all hold a research attitude, they linger and return to view for more than two or three hours. In recent days, groups from Nanjing, Wuxi, Suzhou, and Hangzhou have sent letters requesting an extension of the exhibition. Therefore, it has been decided to extend the exhibition until 8:00 PM on the 19th of this month (Sunday).

Extortionists Ma Bosun Confess to Crimes

Ma Bosun, the grandson of Ma Fengbo, a throat doctor at 902 Haining Road, has recently received threatening letters from gangs, attempting to extort six thousand yuan. Ma reported the case to the French Concession Police. Under the investigation of Chinese Detective Shang Wu, Detective Li Wenbin, and others, five suspects, Wang Yiting, Wang Sanzi, Chen Genlin, Sun Xiaomao, and Zhang Gensheng, were arrested and sent to the First Special District Court for detention. Details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Tan Xinzhen continued the trial in the Eighth Criminal Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin filed a public prosecution according to Article 346, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, for the crime of attempted extortion by intimidation, requesting that they be punished according to the law. Wang Yiting and Wang Sanzi both confessed to writing threatening letters, admitting to intending to extort Ma Bosun. Chen Genlin, Sun Xiaomao, and Zhang Gensheng all denied the charges. After Judge Tan reviewed the confessions, he announced the conclusion of the hearing and awaited sentencing.

Hua Manager Xu Wenliang of Mei Foo Oil Company Kidnapped. Bandits Climbed Over Short Wall, Opened Gate, Drove Car into Garden, Robbed Cash, Foreign Currency, and Jewelry, Then Abducted Xu. Bandits' Fingerprints and Footprints Were All Taken.

Xu Wenliang, a Cantonese, 40 years old, residing at 1305 Yuyuan Road, is the Hua Manager of Mei Foo Oil Company in this city. At about 2:00 AM yesterday morning, while Xu and his wife were fast asleep, a brown rental car with license number 3067 suddenly came to the front of his residence. Unexpectedly, six or seven bandits were ambushed in the car, wearing white and gray short shirts and pants, and black silk shirts and trousers. As soon as the car stopped in front of the gate, the bandits got out of the car, climbed over the short wall of the gate, removed the door latch from the inside, and opened the gate. One of the bandits drove the car into the garden, then went to knock on the second door, falsely claiming to be a visitor. The servants of the house heard the noise and did not suspect anything, so they opened the door and invited them in. Who knew that everyone was armed? They first shouted at the servants and drove them to a corner to watch. Other bandits rushed upstairs at this time and went to Xu's bedroom. At the same time, Xu and his wife heard chaotic footsteps downstairs and were about to go downstairs to check when they encountered the bandits. Therefore, they were taken captive, forced back into the room, and ordered to open the dresser drawer. First, they robbed more than 400 yuan in cash and foreign currency. At that time, Xu also had relatives, Mrs. Liang and her nephew Xu Chengyuan, in the room. Seeing that Xu's wife and Mrs. Liang were wearing diamond rings on their hands, the bandits insisted on taking them off and put them in their pockets. At that time, the bandits were afraid that someone would come out of the room and shout, so they stuffed everyone in the room with cotton and tied their limbs tightly with hemp ropes, confining them in the room. At the same time, they crowded Xu Wenliang downstairs, pushed him into the car, and fled westward. At that time, those who were confined in the room upstairs suddenly heard a gunshot downstairs, and then it was silent. After the bandits had gone far away, Xu's wife and others were untied by the servants and regained their freedom. They went downstairs to look for Xu Wenliang, but he was nowhere to be found. It was undoubtedly a kidnapping. They immediately telegraphed the Jing'an Temple Police Station to request assistance. The police, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to rush to investigate. A pool of blood was found next to the lower steps of the handrail, and a bullet was recovered. Footprints were all over the lawn, and they were taken one by one for tracking. The bullet was also taken back for filing. It was learned that the kidnappers all spoke with a Jiangbei accent. As for the bandit vehicle No. 3067, it was found near Jing'an Temple at about 4:00 AM. There were many fingerprints and footprints left on the car, which were also photographed one by one for filing.

Salt Merchant Zhou Mingjiu Accused by Widow of Seduction and Abandonment. Plaintiff Requests to Withdraw Complaint, Not Approved. After Trial, Ordered to Settle Out of Court Within Seven Days.

Zhou Mingjiu, a salt merchant from Anhui residing in Shanghai, 48 years old, residing at No. 12 Lianzhuli, Avenue Edward VII, has recently been accused in the First Special Court by Ouyang Bibo, a widow from Xiangyang, Hunan, through lawyer Peng Jianxun, of criminal charges of seduction and pregnancy, intentional abandonment, requesting that he be punished according to the law. The indictment briefly stated that the plaintiff is 34 years old, residing at No. 429 Bubai Road in the French Concession, married to a man surnamed Chen, who died eight years ago. To maintain her livelihood, she is a teacher at the Bomei Embroidery School on Avenue Edward VII. In April of last year, she met the defendant on the road. After his repeated pursuits, they became friends. Later, on August 16th, she was deceived and lost her virginity at the Xintai Hotel in Hangzhou. Now the plaintiff is eight months pregnant, and the defendant has abandoned her. Therefore, she filed a lawsuit. This case has been summoned by the Special Court once. Because the defendant did not arrive, the court ordered a change of date for another hearing. Details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhong Qing continued the trial in the Second Criminal Court. The defendant Zhou Mingjiu also arrived in court with his lawyer. The plaintiff's attorney stated that the case was being mediated by relatives and friends during the rescheduling, and the plaintiff was nearly full-term in her pregnancy and eager to return to her hometown, so she did not want to be involved in litigation and requested to withdraw the case. Judge Zhong stated that according to Article 294 of the indictment, it is not a crime that can be prosecuted upon complaint and cannot be withdrawn according to regulations. He then began the trial. The defendant Zhou Mingjiu confessed that in April of last year, he was eating snacks in a coffee shop when the plaintiff came to shop, so they met and became friends. At that time, the plaintiff lived in the Tianjin Apartment and repeatedly invited him to go there, so he went to talk. Later, a physical relationship occurred in a Hangzhou inn, but they did not rent a house together, so there was no possibility of abandonment. He could not admit the pregnancy of the plaintiff, and he already had a wife at home. The court asked why the defendant still behaved absurdly outside since he had a wife. The defendant replied that this was just a moment of confusion and requested understanding. The plaintiff Ouyang Bibo then stated that the case was currently being mediated by relatives and friends, and she was eager to return home to give birth, so she requested instructions. Judge Zhong ordered the case to be rescheduled and ordered both parties to reconcile out of court. If a reconciliation is reached within seven days, a statement should be submitted to the court, otherwise a judgment will be made again.

Tu Xiaoying and Daughter Accuse Tong Rongsong of Seduction and Forgery. 2,000 Yuan Passbook Forged from 100 Yuan. Court Investigated Bank and Obtained Truth. Debate Concluded Yesterday, Sentencing Scheduled.

Tong Rongsong, a young man from Jiangdu, 19 years old, is the son-in-law of Sun of the Dalun Woolen Shop on Qipan Street. Recently, Tu Xiaoying (also known as Meizhen), a Ningbo woman residing at No. 19 Jinye Lane, Weihai Road, was accused by her mother, Tu Chenshi, and her uncle, Tu Jianren, of seduction and forgery in the First Special Court, as well as an additional civil lawsuit for 20,000 yuan. Judge Tan Xinzhen summoned them several times. Because the plaintiff originally pointed out that the 2,000 yuan passbook issued by the defendant by the China Industrial Bank was forged from one yuan, it was necessary to investigate this point with the bank. Therefore, the defendant was ordered to pay a 5,000 yuan bond for release pending trial. Details have been reported in this newspaper. At 11:20 AM yesterday morning, Judge Tan continued the trial in the Eighth Criminal Court and repeatedly questioned the defendant Tong Rongsong about the date and amount of the deposit. According to Tong, the total amount of the passbook was 300 yuan, which was deposited in January of last year. Later, because Tu Xiaoying borrowed money from me, the two of them were very close at the time, so I gave her the passbook at the Victory Ballroom on Beijing Road. However, no one else was present to see it. Tu Xiaoying was indeed a dancer who worked at the Dahuhui, Wellington, and other ballrooms. When I met her, it was at the Victory Ballroom, etc. According to Tu Xiaoying, the passbook stated 2,000 yuan, which was given on May 15th of this year, and I am not a dancer. I have never been to the Victory Ballroom. I only went to the New World Company's International Ballroom with the defendant. I now request that the defendant be punished according to the law. As for the additional civil lawsuit, her lawyer requested to withdraw it so that she could file a separate lawsuit in the civil court in the future. Judge Tan stated that according to the China Industrial Bank's reply, the amount on the passbook was indeed 300 yuan, which was deposited on February 18th of last year, and 200 yuan was withdrawn on the 21st, leaving 100 yuan. Therefore, the defendant's statement that the date of payment of the passbook was after the withdrawal of 200 yuan does not match the facts. At this point, the case was clear. After the lawyers for both parties debated, the court ordered a change of date for sentencing.

Borrowing a Long Gown to Pawn for Prostitution. Two Lowlifes Fight. Two People Covered in Blood Arrested.

Rogue Fang Baoqing, 24 years old, from Ningbo, residing at No. 11 Lixian Lane, Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, and Zhang Laoer, 28 years old, from Haimen, residing at No. 1 Jingyi Lane, Malang Road, are both lowlifes in the Baoyuli area of Dongxinqiao in the French Concession. At the beginning of this month, Zhang borrowed a long gown from Fang Baoqing for urgent needs and pawned it. It was learned that the clothes Zhang borrowed and pawned were used by Hu Tiao women and could not be redeemed for a long time, so he was trapped in a small inn every day and could not go out. As a result, the two became enemies and had a verbal dispute once. At about 2:00 AM yesterday morning, the two sides gathered more than a dozen people and fought in Baoyuli, Dongxinqiao Street. Fang Baoqing first used a sharp axe to chop Zhang Laoer's right arm. Zhang, in pain, seized the axe from Fang's hand and chopped Fang's leg twice. At that time, Lu Zhonglian came out to mediate, and they did not report the arrest. When the two were walking together on the grass east of the Zhongnan Hotel on Avenue Edward VII in the Public Concession, the patrolmen saw that Fang and Zhang were covered in blood and took them to the police station. Later, Zhang was seriously injured and was ordered to be sent to the hospital for treatment. Fang was slightly injured and temporarily detained. After learning that the location of the incident was in the French Concession, the French police were notified to send detectives to investigate.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast for 4:00 PM yesterday stated that there would be halo phenomena around the sun, indicating a northwest wind and showers, due to the passage of a low-pressure system towards Liaodong. The middle reaches of the Yellow River were relatively good with a northwest wind. There was thunder in the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River, along with a northeast wind. The wind direction in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River was variable and the weather was gradually improving. There were strong southwest to northwest winds in the East China Sea and Taiwan Strait, with local rain. Also, the highest temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 93.0 degrees, and the lowest was 75.0 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 100.8 degrees and the lowest was 78.6 degrees.

Report on Industrial and Commercial Changes in Shanghai in the First Quarter of This Year - Edited by China Credit Information (XXXII of Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview)

The following table summarizes the general situation of the rise and fall of Shanghai's industry and commerce in the first three months of this year, compared with the same period last year, according to the statistics obtained from our institute's survey:

Observing the table above, the figures for various changes in the first quarter of the twenty-fifth year are larger than those in the same period of the twenty-fourth year. There are two reasons for this: one is that the industrial and commercial changes themselves this year are indeed greater than last year, and the other is that our institute's survey work and material collection work are better than before. As for the meaning of the column, expansion and contraction refer to the increase or decrease in the business scope of an enterprise. For example, an increase in capital or the establishment of a branch belongs to expansion, while the shutdown of machinery or the withdrawal of share capital belongs to contraction. If the change also involves a change of owner or name, it is classified under reorganization. In the statistics of our institute in the twenty-fourth year, these two changes were not specifically separated, so the figures are lacking. It does not mean that there were no such changes in the same period last year. (To be continued)

Special Issue of Shen Bao on National Products

The Three Major Forces of the Summer Student National Products Movement

— Yao Mingran

(1) Self-Reflection: Zengzi said, "I examine myself three times a day." Self-reflection can indeed lead to repentance and awareness of mistakes, which is the foundation for developing good habits. I have been using national products paper to write manuscripts for three years. At first, I also used imported goods that were not national products. Once I reflected on myself and realized it was not right, I immediately switched to using national products paper. This shows that as long as you reflect on yourself, any problem can be solved. Students are the backbone of society. In today's deeply troubled national situation, if they do not reflect and switch to using national products, then what else can be said? I think all students, whether in elementary, middle, or high school, should have this concept, using their strength to change the wrong path of using non-national products. This is the so-called heart-changing movement that fundamentally solves the problem in the current promotion of the summer student national products movement, so that we will not repeat past mistakes.

(2) Chain Reaction: Self-reflection alone is only the first stage of an individual using national products. Fortunately, students are in the initial stage of group life. I think friends who meet morning and evening should take responsibility together, using a chain reaction method to persuade each other to use national products. At the same time, the school should notify parents to work together. This will not be without some effect. The goal of national products is that students use national products. Students are not merchants blinded by profit and are easy to unite and reject foreign goods. However, this precious enthusiasm cannot be sustained without the support of principals and parents. To achieve this step, there must be a three-in-one chain reaction force of students, parents, and principals to be effective!

(3) Organizational Power: As mentioned above, a three-in-one force is necessary to achieve the goal of students using national products. But what is the use of not holding it enthusiastically? Isn't that just a bubble? Therefore, the allocation of organizational power is the main base camp for accomplishing this goal. I hope that if we do nothing, then so be it, but if we do, we must have the spirit of seeing it through from beginning to end, and the perseverance to make some achievements and models to show students who do not use national products. We do not use empty words, we only speak of a few points. To be honest, to achieve this major responsibility, we must ask the Summer Student National Products Movement Association to work with the Education Bureau to jointly handle it. I hope that in the future it will not be limited to the summer vacation, and it is best to have grades like homework, so that students can wake up. If this step cannot be implemented, I think there will be no effect!

A Word of Contribution

Sending Off the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group

— Yang An

The Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group, under the leadership of the China Industrial Foreign Trade Association, will embark on a long journey of thousands of miles tomorrow. What a magnificent trip! As a reporter, on the occasion of your departure, I respectfully offer this word of advice, as a small expression of my sincerity.

The gentlemen of the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group are all powerful members of the national products industry, with experience in industrial manufacturing and export promotion. Based on their long-standing enthusiasm for national products, they will deeply investigate the actual situation of Nanyang trade, demonstrate the truth about national products and the contents of various factories, carry more than 300 boxes of samples, conduct large-scale publicity, and make extremely sincere connections. The impact on the export of national products is immeasurable.

Gentlemen, you should understand that Nanyang is of great importance to our country, and Japanese spies are eager for Nanyang. If our national products industry and Nanyang overseas Chinese do not have the determination to cooperate and fight to strengthen the strength of foreign trade, then our country's commercial position in Nanyang will soon disappear. Gentlemen, this trip should be with the determination to expand the field of national products, not just for ordinary socializing. As I see it, there are three things to avoid on this trip, and four things to emphasize. What are the three things to avoid?

(1) Avoid Meaningless Socializing: The inspection time is extremely short. It is certainly not acceptable to rush through it superficially. It is difficult to know the actual situation without long-term visits and extremely precise investigations. Therefore, meaningless socializing should be reduced or avoided as much as possible.

(2) Avoid Indulgent Behavior: The Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group is going abroad for the first time. All eyes are on you. If your behavior is improper, it will not only give overseas Chinese something to criticize, but also lose the trust of the people of Nanyang. Therefore, every move should respect the status of a national member and maintain the reputation of the country. All speeches and talks should be based on the overall position, not on trivialities, and should not be done independently.

(3) Avoid Perfunctory Work: The biggest problem with inspection groups in the past has been perfunctory work. After a superficial inspection, the excitement fades away. Everyone goes back to their own business and forgets about it. This kind of inspection is worthless. Therefore, we should work hard, thoroughly implement the plan, and maintain it from beginning to end with determination. After the inspection, there should be opportunities for contact and room for work at all times, correcting the past malpractices to great benefit.

What are the four things to emphasize?

(1) It is necessary to establish national products exhibition halls in major Nanyang cities with local chambers of commerce, to display the national product samples sent there for a long time, so as to show them to overseas Chinese and provide a constant reference. At the same time, we should promote the new and remove the old, and replace them from time to time.

(2) It is necessary to establish an introduction office in major Nanyang cities in conjunction with overseas Chinese to handle the introduction of national products and be responsible for answering inquiries from overseas Chinese in various places.

(3) It is necessary to establish a national products sales office or a Chinese national products company in major Nanyang cities with overseas Chinese or chambers of commerce, so that overseas Chinese can recognize national products and feel more affinity, and the sales of national products can be further expanded.

(4) It is necessary to establish a joint operations center for Shanghai national products factories in major Nanyang cities, gathering dozens of factories and inviting someone who is familiar with the Nanyang situation and has experience in sales to stay in Nanyang to preside over everything, so as to facilitate communication and boost sales.

This trip will complete Nanyang commercial shipping and establish a Nanyang bank, all in order to promote the development of Nanyang commerce and provide opportunities for the smooth sale of national products. The relationship of this trip is truly crucial. I also offer a word to wish you victory.

Contributions to the Student Summer National Products Promotion Group

— Xiao Shi

Patriotic students, in this hot summer, you have accepted the resolution of the National Products Movement United Association of this city, organized the Student Summer National Products Promotion Group, and gone to the interior to carry out advocacy. On the one hand, you are displaying your patriotic spirit, and on the other hand, you are awakening society. This is truly a great value and far-reaching significance! How to promote? How to guide? There will be very detailed regulations, which I need not repeat. What I want to contribute to the students is the several issues that should be paid attention to when promoting.

1. Be Popular: The minds of the people in the interior are very simple, their knowledge is very shallow, and any strangeness in their actions and clothing can arouse their suspicion. If you are wearing and using one or two kinds of non-national products, or even most of them are non-national products, no matter how eloquent you are or how great a speaker you are, I am afraid that as soon as you open your mouth, people behind you will be criticizing you for being hypocritical. If you don't even know how to love your country, how can you be qualified to persuade others to love their country? This point is important. If you don't pay attention to it beforehand, the result will be futile, or even leave a very bad impression.

2. Go Deep into Public Opinion: In big cities and towns, everything is more easily noticed. When we promote national products, we should pay more attention to the masses who do not know or are unaware. To reach the masses who do not know or are unaware, we must go deep into public opinion. In this hot weather, going deep into public opinion is indeed very troublesome. Transportation is inconvenient, and living and eating are mostly simple. Without the habit of being able to endure hardship, I am afraid that you will not be able to bear this responsibility. Now, private goods have penetrated deeply into public opinion. In remote areas, you can encounter peddlers selling smuggled goods everywhere. To eliminate smuggled goods, how can we not track smuggled goods and go deep into the people?

3. Don't Complain About Hardship: Serving society and enduring hardship is common, but sometimes it can even make you suffer grievances for no reason. When we speak to the public, it is really difficult to predict whether it will be effective or not. If you are not careful, you may even be reprimanded to your face or suffer insulting words, which is extremely common in the uneducated interior. We must pay attention to it at all times, and even if we encounter it unfortunately, we should deal with it calmly. We should consider it as an expected occurrence of being wronged for no reason. If you cannot tolerate it, either the plan will fail or troubles will arise. Therefore, when you go out to promote, on the one hand, you must be able to endure hardship, and on the other hand, you must have a big belly to tolerate nonsense.

Sports News

World Games Torch Relay Race Scheduled to Depart from Athens on the 20th. It Must Travel Eleven Days and Nights to Reach the Berlin Venue. There Will Be an Extremely Grand and Solemn Ceremony at the Departure.

Athens, July 13 (Havas Agency) The 11th Olympic Games will soon open in Berlin. Crown Prince Paul will represent the Greek Olympic Committee to attend. The local authorities have decided that on the 20th of this month, the Olympic torch will be relayed from the holy city of Altis (the site of the ancient Olympic Games) by relay runners to Berlin. The section from the holy city of Aritis to the Bulgarian border is 1,108 kilometers long. 1,108 local athletes will be responsible for the relay, with each person responsible for one kilometer. When it reaches the Bulgarian border, it will be relayed by Bulgarian athletes until it reaches Berlin.

Athens, July 13 (National Sealand Agency) At the opening of the World Games, a torch relay race will start from the altar of the ancient Mount Olympus in ancient Athens, taking eleven days and nights, traveling 3,055 kilometers through seven countries to reach the Berlin venue of this World Games. The Greek athletes participating in this torch relay race received their final training here yesterday. Before the first torchbearer sets off from Mount Olympus, there will be an extremely solemn ceremony. Greek Deputy Minister George Gopulos will represent the Greek government to participate. The torch will be lit in front of the Temple of Zeus by collecting sunlight with a concave mirror. Fourteen young girls will hold the torch and circle the forest around the altar in front of the temple for a week in a solemn atmosphere and reach a specially built altar. They will then stop and hand the torch to the first runner. Before the runner sets off, he will recite the Olympic oath of the Olympic Games and at the same time recite the speech of Count Coubertin, the founder of the modern Olympic Games. Then the bugler will signal the start of the race. The Greek runners will run from Mount Olympus to the Bulgarian border. The route traveled by Greek athletes is 1,108 kilometers, so 1,108 runners are needed.

Newspapers claim that the Greek Crown Prince will participate in the Berlin World Games as the President of the Greek Olympic Committee.

Our Country's Soccer Team's European Tour

— Written and Sent by Team Captain Li Huitang

Rangoon, 8th (Continued)

(June 26) This morning, I read in the Chinese and Western newspapers that the number of spectators yesterday was actually 23,000. They greatly praised our spirit, morality, and soccer skills, which was unprecedented in Rangoon. However, the strength of the Rifle British Army team here is not yet at its peak. The next two matches, one against the local champion and one against a select team, will show what our soccer skills are really like. I haven't seen them yet. I heard that this soccer road is very different from the British Army's sweeping style. The overseas Chinese community is very earnestly reporting the strengths and weaknesses of the opposing team to us, and their concern for us is even greater than our own team's caution. At 2 PM this afternoon, we attended a tea party hosted by the Jinan University Alumni Association, with music to add to the fun. Several members of our team are Jinan University alumni, including Xu Yahui, Chen Zhenhe, and Liang Shutang, which made us feel even closer. After the meeting, we were invited to tour the city's scenery. Along the way, we saw the Golden Pagoda (also known as the Great Pagoda). The top of the pagoda is painted with real gold, which is worth a fortune. You must be barefoot when entering. Inside, there are many statues of gods, mostly decorated with gold. Those who come to Rangoon must visit here for a new perspective. We stayed in our residence and didn't go out in the evening, preparing for tomorrow's fierce battle.

(June 27) Today was our first match in Rangoon, against the Myanmar Police Team, the local champion. They are a strong team and one of the most famous in Southeast Asia. As soon as we arrived here, the overseas Chinese community expected us to defeat this stubborn enemy, and fans from all over were eager to see these two heroes meet. No wonder, when our team arrived at the stadium, nearly half the people were standing outside the gate and couldn't get in for almost half an hour. The crowding inside and outside broke the Rangoon record. There were too many fans in the stadium, who even squeezed into the lines of the field by more than a dozen layers. The spectators in the stands couldn't see the whole picture. The authorities hadn't anticipated this overflow beforehand and weren't prepared, leading to chaos that affected the soccer match. I heard that some people bought tickets at noon and waited inside for five hours. You can imagine their scramble. Their infatuation is even more pitiful. We lost 0-1 in the first half, and won 3-1 in the end. The scorers were Jiang Bo, Beihua, and Jiliang, one each. We slightly changed our formation and calculated as follows:

Bao Jiaping

Cai Wenli, Li Tiansheng

Chen Zhenhe, Liang Rongzhao, Zhang Xianyuan

Zheng Jiliang, Ye Beihua, Li Huitang, Tan Jiangbo, Cao Guicheng

As soon as the silver whistle blew, the Burmese people cheered and shouted for their team, encouraging them. When their team went on the attack, they were extremely agile, with flexible short passes and fierce offensives. In the first fifteen minutes, the soccer ball flew back and forth between the two teams, as fast as shooting stars, which was rare in all the matches. Our team defended more than attacked, resisting tenaciously. Finally, in the twenty-second minute, due to Wenli's inadequate defense, the enemy's right wing calmly crossed the ball, and their center forward flicked it in for the first score. At that time, there was a clap of thunder, and applause and screams mixed together, echoing through the clouds. Afterwards, the enemy's offensive was still fierce. Although we occasionally made advances, we always failed. Fortunately, the first half ended without us losing any more goals. During the break, because our team's performance was very chaotic and we were too focused on controlling the ball, we fell into the enemy's trap of agile passes. So we discussed the best way to deal with them in the second half. After the change of formation, our strategy changed, and our momentum was very different from before. In less than five minutes, Guicheng's precise shot and Jiang Bo's great header equalized the score. The overseas Chinese fans cheered repeatedly. Before long, Huitang got the ball in the middle, passed three defenders in a row, and shot fiercely with his right foot. The ball bounced off the goalkeeper's body. Fortunately, Beihua sprinted quickly, charged alone, and lightly flicked it in. Only then did the overseas Chinese compatriots smile. The other team's offensive in the first half was too fierce, and their defense was too tiring. In the second half, they lacked energy, and their offense and defense were relaxed, unlike the fierce attacks in the first half. Near the end of the match, Jiliang lay in wait on the left wing, waiting for Guicheng's cross from the middle. Like an arrow shot from a drawn bow, he volleyed, and after it went into the net, the goalkeeper was still as still as a wooden chicken. The match ended 3-1. The overseas Chinese compatriots all felt satisfied. Our team lost first in the first half, which was the first time we had been defeated on this southern tour. In the thirty minutes of battle, the other team definitely had the upper hand. It was very fortunate that we were able to defend and not lose too much. In the second half, our team's sleeping lion had awakened, and our measures were effective. In addition, the opponent's fatigue gradually appeared, and they couldn't hold on. If their goalkeeper hadn't had repeated luck, they would have lost more than three goals. The other team's strength was indeed extraordinary. Their coordination, short passes, control, footwork, and positioning were all excellent. Both wings were very active. The only thing they lacked was the final blow, which they didn't have a firm grip on. Every time they had a chance, they always missed it in an instant. Shooting is not easy. Everywhere we have been, we have felt that there are very few people who are skilled in this area. If we had lost one more goal in the first half, what would the result have been? I really don't want to imagine it. The fierceness and tension of the battle, and the danger of our position, made me feel a lingering fear after the fact. Our team played the enemy's fast game in the first half, which was unwise. In addition, Jiang Bo's leg was injured by the enemy, and he repeatedly wanted to seek revenge, so he couldn't focus all his attention on the game. It was not without reason that the forwards couldn't score on the field. Fortunately, he was teachable. In the second half, he didn't act impulsively. He scored the first goal with a header, which was a rare achievement. Jiang Bo's head is not easy to come by. The British consider it to be top-notch, and it's not an exaggeration. I alone scored five goals in the first half, becoming the target of everyone's attacks, which was expected. However, in the second half, I was still able to advance when the opportunity arose, repeatedly entering the enemy's territory, and posing a great threat to the enemy's defenders, causing them to be distracted. Wenli hadn't been on the field for a long time, and he felt unfamiliar at first, but he gradually got into the game. Tiansheng was one of the best performers on this southern tour, and his skills in tackling, hooking, and stealing were all excellent, earning him a lot of praise. Rongzhao, after Yahui got sick, took over the defense in the middle and also made significant progress. The rest of the players, except for Beihua, who hasn't recovered his former form, were all able to work hard and put on a good performance. Guicheng ran fast, making the enemy look like children, which also made the people here clap their hands and sigh. If he could train his stamina, then Guicheng is not old yet.

Educational News

The Sixth Annual Meeting of the Chinese Children's Education Society Was Held in Lushan; Cheng Bolu, Chen Heqin, Dong Renjian, etc. Presided and Reported; This Year's Meeting Focused on Group Meetings and Academic Discussions

The Sixth Annual Meeting of the Chinese Children's Education Society was held at the Lushan Library from the 10th to the 13th of this month. The opening ceremony was held at 9 AM on the 10th, with more than 200 member representatives present. The presidium included Cheng Bolu, Chen Heqin, Dong Renjian, Cheng Qibao, Li Qingsong, Ma Ketan, and Yu Ziyi. The ceremony was conducted according to protocol.

Chen Heqin's Address

Next, Chen Heqin reported on the Society's affairs, stating in essence that the Chinese Children's Education Society started from the Nanjing Gulou Kindergarten. Since 1929, in a few years, the number of members has reached more than 3,000, with 17 branches and 13 working districts established. In terms of work, the Society focuses on academic research. The reading group of the Shanghai branch has held 63 meetings and published publications such as the Children's Education Monthly and annual reports, as well as 36 series of books. It is also planning to publish 1,000 series of books in the next three years. In addition, it is collecting children's education books for members to read and sending members to conduct field surveys at home and abroad. In terms of funding, the subsidies from various sources and membership fees are sufficient for application. As for the Society's goals for future efforts, the first is to enable children to fully develop their bodies and minds under the current national situation, the second is to promote the movement of building the country with good teachers, and finally, to express gratitude to the local party and government officials and the gentlemen of the preparatory committee.

Xie Yinian's Report

Next, Xie Yinian, representative of the preparatory committee, reported on the preparation process, first stating the unique points of this year's annual meeting compared to previous annual meetings: (1) Previous annual meetings focused on the reading of papers, while this year's meeting focuses on group discussions; (2) Previous annual meetings invited representatives from various academic institutions in China to participate in the meeting, while this year's meeting focuses on the exchange of academics; (3) At this year's annual meeting, each branch and each working district sent representatives to participate and jointly discuss the methods for carrying out the affairs of each place; (4) This year's annual meeting does not focus on serious formal discussions, but on the unity of spirit and will. Next, he said that the work of the preparatory committee failed to do everything perfectly and hoped that the members would understand and forgive.

Cheng Bolu's Speech

Next, Cheng, Director of the Jiangxi Education Department, gave a speech, the main idea of which was that this year's annual meeting of the Chinese Children's Education Society in Lushan has three special meanings: (1) The Chinese Children's Education Society has made special contributions to Chinese children's education; (2) Lushan is a famous scenic spot in the world and a Chinese park. China has been dominated by Buddhist, Neo-Confucian, and modern cultural spirits for thousands of years. Lushan has the combination of the Lotus Society for Buddhist research, the Zhu Xi lectures at the White Deer Cave for Neo-Confucianism, and the foreign missionaries studying religion in Guling for modern culture. The Chinese Children's Education Society should carry on the past and open up to create Lushan's fourth period of culture; (3) The special significance of the conference itself is to emphasize academic discussion and the unity of spiritual will.

In addition, he has three hopes for the Chinese Children's Education Society: (1) He hopes that the conference will focus on discussing problems, and that solutions can be found for compulsory education, children's health, labor education, science education, and education in extraordinary times. Special attention should also be paid to the training of teachers themselves; (2) He hopes to promote the atmosphere of academic research. The Chinese Children's Education Society is the authority on children's education in the country and should take on the responsibility of shifting the social atmosphere and promoting academic research; (3) He hopes that the members of the Chinese Children's Education Society will deeply recognize the demands of the times and that all aspects of life will be militarized. Under the firm belief of building the country with good teachers, establish several creeds, be determined and unremitting, in order to realize it. Later, Tan Bingxun, director of the Administration Bureau, gave a speech.

After the opening of the conference, all the members were divided into 14 small groups, and each group held a friendship meeting to report on the status of the schools served by the members, the research experience, and various practical problems, and to seek solutions. In the afternoon, group discussion meetings were held, divided into (1) Elementary School Administration, (2) Elementary School Teaching, and (3) Early Childhood Education. Dozens of proposals from various provinces were submitted one by one for discussion and obtained considerable results.

Pinghu Recruits Elementary School Teachers, Penalizes Those Who Do Not Participate in Centralized Training

The centralized training for elementary school teachers and staff in Pinghu County opened on the 10th. The county government, in view of the fact that some elementary school principals and teachers have used excuses to evade or disobey and not attend the training, has decided to impose dismissal penalties in accordance with regulations and suspend their employment for three years. To fill the vacancies, 20 qualified personnel will be recruited. The age requirement is 20 to 40 years old. Qualifications include graduation from a junior high school or above, or having served as an elementary school teacher for five years or more. The registration period is from now until the 15th. The registration procedure is to fill out the registration form and submit proof documents. The examination date is 8 AM on July 16th. The written test subjects are Chinese language and educational science (writing supplies must be brought by the applicant). The registration location is the centralized training class for elementary school teachers and staff in the east courtyard of Danghu Elementary School. After being admitted, they must participate in centralized training, and their treatment will be the same as that of the students currently being trained (food and lodging will be provided by the class). After the training period expires, those who pass the examination and assessment will be assigned to various schools.

The Jicha Political Council Provides Relief to Unemployed University Graduates

(Beiping, Central News Agency, 14th) Qin Decheng talked about the fact that there are many unemployed university graduates in Ping and Jing. The Political Council has decided on relief measures. A committee will be formed soon to implement examinations, paying attention to (1) those who are healthy, (2) those who have a foundation in Chinese studies, and (3) those who have specialized knowledge. After being admitted, they will be assigned to work in various institutions in Pingjin and Jicha.

(Nanjing, 14th) The provisional higher examination will be held on September 10th and will end on the 20th. Chen Daqi will serve as the director of the Examination Affairs Office. He Tingsheng and others, university graduates in Ping, have formulated many opinions on the employment of university graduates and presented them to the Executive Yuan on the 14th. The Yuan sent a staff member to reply: (1) The government is very concerned about the employment of university graduates and is preparing measures to broaden their opportunities; (2) The Executive Yuan has agreed with the Examination Yuan to hold a higher civil service examination this year. The timing of the examination has been set; (3) The Executive Yuan is currently negotiating with the Central Political School to run a vocational training class for graduates with specialized degrees or higher, recruiting 1,000 people to attend the class; (4) Specialized technical students from various agencies will be employed as appropriate.

Analysis of National Compulsory Education Funding; Over 4.7 Million Yuan This Year

In the past, the funding for compulsory education in various provinces and cities across the country was mostly raised by the provinces, cities, and local areas themselves, which hindered its full development. Since the 24th year of the Republic, the central government has included 2.4 million yuan in the national treasury budget to subsidize compulsory education funding in various provinces and cities, leading the way. With the addition of funding raised by provinces, cities, and counties themselves, progress in the implementation of compulsory education has been steadily increasing through this dual approach. In the 24th year of the Republic, the central government's payment for national compulsory education funding was 2.4 million yuan. The Sino-British, Sino-French, Sino-American, and Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Funds were originally intended to be subsidized by the central education authorities with 800,000 yuan, totaling 3.2 million yuan. However, after discussion, only the Sino-French and Sino-American Boxer Indemnity Funds provided subsidies, totaling 300,000 yuan. Therefore, the central government's compulsory education funding in the 24th year of the Republic was nominally 3.2 million yuan, but in reality, it was only 2.7 million yuan. This year's (25th year) central budget includes 5 million yuan for education construction and 500,000 yuan for border education, totaling 5.5 million yuan. After deducting 1.1 million yuan for operating mass schools, compiling supplementary reading materials for the masses, and for educational films and radio education (how this 1.1 million yuan will be allocated will be decided by the education authorities in a meeting soon), there remains 4.4 million yuan. With the addition of 150,000 yuan from the Sino-American Boxer Indemnity Fund, 50,000 yuan from the Sino-French Boxer Indemnity Fund, and over 100,000 yuan from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund (the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund, including subsidies for middle schools, totals 200,000 yuan, with the larger subsidy for compulsory education being between 120,000 and 150,000 yuan), the total is over 4.7 million yuan for the central government's compulsory education funding in the 25th year. It is reported that the central education authorities have already held a meeting and decided to allocate 4.6 million yuan to subsidize various provinces, cities, and border areas for the implementation of compulsory education. The remaining tens of thousands of yuan will be used for expenses related to compulsory education experiments, equipment, and supervision. The specific amounts of compulsory education funding that each province, city, and district should receive from the central government will be communicated to the provinces, cities, and districts by the responsible education authorities via telegram.

Finance: Spot Gold Premium Drops Again by One Yuan and One Cent; Futures Premium Only Rises by Slightly More Than Three Yuan

The gold market was weak after an initial calm yesterday, resulting in sideways movement. Supply and demand within the market were relatively balanced, but due to spot premium swap activities, short selling seemed active, continuing to push prices lower. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets saw London rise and the US remain flat. Monte Carlo forward silver prices rose by between five haos and two and a half percent. Exchange rates narrowed, and London spot gold rose by half a penny. The central bank's listed price was announced to be 1128 yuan. Pre-market trading opened at a weak 33 yuan, but lacked significant impact. The morning opening was slightly lower, and the market immediately went down due to oversupply. However, buying activity emerged after the dip, leading to a brief rebound. HSBC's listed prices for gold and ginger remained flat. The market remained weak, and the silver equalization tax was announced to have risen by half a cent. After this, the situation was calm, hovering around 32 yuan for quite some time. However, the afternoon closing trend was still difficult to boost. The overall market was narrow because futures and spot prices were close. Currently, the premium is only slightly more than 3 yuan, and it is predicted that the current spot premium swap will be no more than that. Both long and short positions are taking a wait-and-see approach. Here is a record of the day's market conditions:

The morning opening was 1132 yuan and 7 jiao, down 1 jiao from the previous close. Luo (brokers) sold a strip at a 1.13 yuan decline, dropping to 1 yuan and 3 jiao. This month's book entry is 1128 yuan, and August's is 1132 yuan. The morning supplementary water (margin call) was 1128 yuan, and pure gold was increased by 8 yuan to 1140 yuan and 7 jiao. The spot market situation was balanced, with Tianjin goods increased by 15 yuan, and boiled red gold increased by 13 yuan, with a lack of sellers. Yarn and Cotton: Local Yarn Trading Too Stagnant; Yarn Market Reveals Weakness; However, There is Still Some Boost This Month, and the Decline is Slightly Reduced

The yarn market is weakening, and the trend of decline is slightly increasing. This is because US cotton continues to fall, causing discouragement, and the current yarn sales market is unusually cold. Customers have no ability to purchase due to high prices. However, the mentality of general speculators is unusually enthusiastic. Considering the good performance of overseas cotton, they blindly advance, and there are rumors that there may be short squeezes in the near month. Unfortunately, local yarn trading is too stagnant, with only 50 bales traded throughout the day, while Japanese yarn trading has more than 300 bales.

#### Forward Months Fall Sharply by Two Yuan

At the pre-noon opening of marked yarn, the market mentality was fatigued due to the continued decline in US cotton. Near-term fell by 1.2 yuan, and forward months fell by 1.45 yuan. The market was weak. After the second session, there were various rumors in the market, saying that the long side was preparing to take delivery of a large quantity of goods and there were short squeeze actions. The August contract suddenly jumped by 1 yuan, and forward months followed, rising by 1 yuan to 6.7 jiao. By the third closing, it was heard that current yarn sales were quiet and local yarn was scarce, and market sentiment turned loose. Although the near month was high, forward months fell sharply by more than 1 yuan. As a result, compared to the previous day's closing price, all months except the near month rose by 4 jiao, and forward months fell sharply by 2 yuan to 2 yuan, 1.4, and 7 jiao. The opening prices of near and far months reversed and weakened. When bidding for September and October contracts, the Three-Piece Yarn of Dagu rose sharply by 3.4 yuan in the near month, and market sentiment was still not aroused. All months rose by 6.7 jiao, but afterward, due to sluggish yarn sales, the near month fell by 6 jiao to 1 yuan compared to the morning closing price, and the forward month rose by 1 jiao. It was found that 1,600 bales of Deda were sold, 1,950 bales of Dafu, 1,200 bales of Tongji, 950 bales of Hengyi, 3,500 bales of Taixing, 2,250 bales of Gengfeng, 1,300 bales of Xingchang, 2,600 bales of Changfeng, 4,950 bales of Runkang, 1,800 bales of Dachang, and 1,100 bales of Xiacheng. 1,350 bales of Juxing, 2,800 bales of Yudai, 900 bales of Yuanda, 1,550 bales of Hexing, 1,400 bales of Fengtai, 4,900 bales of Shenji, 3,850 bales of Dachangcheng, 1,730 bales of Taichang, 1,000 bales of Hengchang, and 1,000 bales of Dachang were bought. #### Current Yarn Sales Clear at Lower Prices

Current yarn sales are very clear. It was found that various merchants bought 387 bales throughout the day, and the selling price fell by 1 yuan. The purchase amount of each merchant is listed below:

Same Industry 155, Wuhu 10, Changsha 5

Inland 205, Ningbo 7, Tianjin 5

Cotton Merchants Sell Short En Masse, Marked Cotton Falls Across the Board

The cotton market saw new and old cotton fall across the board, and momentum was slightly dampened. The drought-stricken area of US cotton received rain, and southern farmers continued to sell short, falling by more than ten pounds. Indian cotton also followed, and market sentiment was discouraged. At the same time, demand for current cotton completely stopped, and everyone sold short. However, the long side's intention remained firm, and the idea of squeezing the old cotton market has not yet been abandoned.

#### Near and Far Months Fall by About Half a Yuan

At the opening of the marked cotton market yesterday, US cotton received rainfall, and southern cotton farmers sold short, falling by 8 to 16 pounds. Indian cotton also fell by 1 Rupee 75. Dagu's Three-Piece Cotton fell by 1.2 yuan in the near month. Market sentiment was average, and buying momentum decreased. The near month fell by 3.5 jiao. When bidding for the August contract, the long side came to pull up again, and the market appeared tight and unmoved. In October, old cotton received the assistance of the long side and suddenly jumped by 2.5 jiao. The August contract was restored to above 50 yuan, but the volume was average. By the closing, the cotton market was weak due to the lack of strength in the yarn market. Some of the profitable long side closed out, and old cotton fell sharply by 3 or 4 jiao. The far month was dragged down by Shanghai. As a result, compared to the previous day's closing price, old cotton fell by 4 to 4.5 jiao, and new cotton fell by 4.5 to 6.8 jiao. At the afternoon opening, old cotton was still exhausted and weak, while new cotton rose by 2 jiao. The third closing was because the Osaka Three-Piece Cotton market turned firm after being weak. The near month jumped sharply by 5.5 jiao, the August contract rose by 2.5 jiao, and new cotton rose by 5 points. As a result, all months rose by 1 jiao compared to the morning closing price. It was found that 3,000 dan of Yuda were sold, 2,500 dan of Yikang, 2,000 dan of Deda, 15,000 dan of Tongji, 12,000 dan of Hengyi, 7,200 dan of Mingde, 4,000 dan of Senkang, 1,600 dan of Changfeng, 2,500 dan of Dachang, 1,500 dan of Changhe, 1,700 dan of Xingchang, 3,700 dan of Changyu, 2,500 dan of Taichang, 2,000 dan of Xiacheng, and 6,000 dan of Shengyuan. 25 dan of Xinchang, 3,000 dan of Juxing, 1,500 dan of Yukang, 3,000 dan of Dafeng, 4,700 dan of Yuanda, 11,000 dan of Hexing, 3,500 dan of Shenchang, 3,500 dan of Ruida, 2,500 dan of Fengtai, 12,500 dan of Shenji, 8,800 dan of Dachangcheng, and 4,000 dan of Runkang were bought.
